 - input bhashaa According to Shivpuran, Bhairava was born on the eighth day of Krishna Paksha of Margashirsha month in the afternoon from the part of Lord Shankar
 isliye is tithi ko kaal bhairavashtami yaa bhairavashtami ke naam se janaa jaataa he
 According to the Puranas, Andhakasura monster once forgot his abilities and attacked Lord Shiva in arrogance
 uske sanhaar ke lieshiv ke khun se bhairav kii utpatti hui
 Kaal Bhairav is the form of Shiva
 isliye shiv kii aradhana se pehle bhairav upasna kaa vidhaan bataaya gaya he
 It is said that his practice gets rid of all sorrows
 kaashi or ujjain ko bhairav kaa siddh sthaan mana jaataa he
 It is said that a person doing Bhairav sadhana gets rid of worldly sufferings
 vaise to pramukhakalashtami kaa vrath kalbhairav jayantike din kiya jaataa he, lekin kalbhairav ke bhakt har maheene hi krishna paksh kii ashtami par inaki puja or archana karte hai or vrath rakhte hai
 It is believed that by observing Kikalabhairava, all the wishes of the worshiper are fulfilled
 vartmaan main bhairav kii upasna batuka bhairav or kaal bhairav ke rup main prachlit hai
 In Tantra Sadhana, worship of eight forms of Bhairava is said
 ye rup asitanga bhairav, rudra bhairav, chandra bhairav, krodh bhairav, unmatta bhairav, kapali bhairav, bheeshan bhairav sanhaar bhairav
 In the Kalika Purana, Bhairav is described as Lord Ganesha, whose vehicle is a dog
 is din vrath rakhane vaale sadhak ko puraa din 'om kalbhairavaay nam:' kaa jaap karnaa chahie
 According to Kalashtami fast, Vidhinarada Purana, Kalakabhairava and mother Durga should be worshiped on the day of Kalashtami

 aaj ke din vrati ko falahar hi karnaa chahie

 kyon rakhaa jaataa he kalashtami kaa vratakatha ke anusaar ek din bhagwaan brahma or vishnu ke bich shreshth hone kaa vivaad utpann hua

 sabhi devataaon or muni kii sahmati seshiv ji ko shresthmana gaya
